         R3: (0, 11) -> (1, 7)   (bridge down from R3_t to R2_s)
         R2: (1, 6) -> (2, 4)   (bridge down from R2_t to R1_s)
         R1: (2, 3) -> (6, 0)
     10. whole: s=(0, 11) -> t=(8, 0)
         R3: (0, 11) -> (1, 7)   (bridge down from R3_t to R2_s)
         R2: (1, 6) -> (2, 4)   (bridge down from R2_t to R1_s)
         R1: (2, 3) -> (8, 0)
